80→\t// In contrast, the Vec behavior in this package is that member extraction before registration\n    81→\t// returns a permanent noop object.\n    82→\n    83→\t// WithLabelValuesChecked, if histograms, gauges) are registered and exposed across three major projects: kubernetes/kubernetes, grafana/grafana, and prometheus/prometheus.\\n\\n### Kubernetes/Kubernetes Pattern\\n\\nKubernetes implements a centralized metrics framework in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/` that abstracts away direct Prometheus dependencies. Key characteristics:\\n\\n1. **Central Registry Abstraction**: `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go` defines a `KubeRegistry` interface that wraps Prometheus registries with custom validation and deprecation tracking. This allows Kubernetes to add custom business logic around metric registration.\\n\\n2. **Legacy Registry Pattern**: `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go` provides a global registry using `RawMustRegister()` for backward compatibility, while newer code uses injected registry instances.\\n\\n3. **Metric Type Wrappers**: Counter, Gauge, and Histogram creation is abstracted through `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/counter.go`, `gauge.go`, and `histogram.go`. These wrappers call `prometheus.NewCounter()`, `prometheus.NewGauge()`, and `prometheus.NewHistogram()` respectively, but add Kubernetes-specific validation.\\n\\n4. **Component-Level Registration**: Each component (controllers, api-server, kubelet, scheduler, proxy) has its own metrics file (e.g., `pkg/controller/cronjob/metrics/metrics.go`, `pkg/scheduler/metrics/metrics.go`) that initializes metrics in init() functions and registers them with either the legacy registry or a KubeRegistry instance. Controllers use `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` while newer components use injected registries.\\n\\n### Grafana/Grafana Pattern\\n\\nGrafana uses a more distributed approach with dependency injection:\\n\\n1. **Metrics Service**: `pkg/infra/metrics/service.go` provides a `MetricsService` that manages prometheus.Registerer and prometheus.Gatherer instances. This service is injected into components that need to register metrics.\\n\\n2. **Distributed Registration**: Unlike Kubernetes's centralized component directories, Grafana's metrics are scattered throughout the codebase. Each service that needs metrics (alerts, dashboards, authentication, storage, etc.) has its own metrics file that receives an injected `prometheus.Registerer` as a dependency.\\n\\n3. **Registration Methods**:\\n   - Direct: `prometheus.MustRegister()` for global metrics\\n   - Injected: `registerer.MustRegister()` for service-specific metrics\\n   - Automatic: `promauto.With(registerer).New*()` for automatic registration with injected registerer\\n   - Conditional: `registerer.Register()` with error handling\\n\\n4. **Examples**:\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/ngalert.go`: NGAlert metrics factory receives a `prometheus.Registerer`\\n   - `pkg/services/dashboards/service/metrics.go`: Dashboard metrics use injected registerer\\n   - `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/metrics.go`: Authentication metrics with dependency injection\\n   - `pkg/services/secrets/manager/metrics.go`: Secrets manager metrics\\n   - `pkg/middleware/request_metrics.go`: HTTP middleware metrics\\n\\n5. **Namespace/Prefix Pattern**: Many Grafana services use `prometheus.WrapRegistererWithPrefix()` to add namespaced prefixes to metrics, creating logical grouping (e.g., \\\"grafana_alerting_\\\", \\\"grafana_dashboard_\\\").\\n\\n### Prometheus/Prometheus Pattern\\n\\nPrometheus itself uses an embedded metrics pattern:\\n\\n1. **No Central Abstraction**: Unlike Kubernetes, Prometheus directly uses the Prometheus Go client library throughout the codebase. There's no intermediate wrapper layer.\\n\\n2. **Distributed Component Metrics**: Metrics are registered in individual components:\\n   - `discovery/metrics.go`: Generic discovery metrics\\n   - `discovery/{consul,dns,kubernetes}/metrics.go`: Service discovery provider-specific metrics\\n   - `scrape/metrics.go`: Scrape manager metrics\\n   - `storage/remote/`: Remote storage client and queue manager metrics\\n   - `tsdb/{db.go,head.go,agent/db.go}`: Time-series database metrics\\n   - `rules/manager.go`: Rule evaluation metrics\\n   - `notifier/metric.go`: Alert notification metrics\\n   - `web/web.go`: HTTP API metrics\\n\\n3. **Registration Pattern**: Each component creates metrics in init() or NewComponent() functions and immediately registers them with `prometheus.MustRegister()` or `registry.MustRegister()` (where registry is passed as parameter or created locally).\\n\\n4. **Examples of Registration**:\\n   - `cmd/prometheus/main.go`: Main process initialization registers all component metrics\\n   - `tsdb/db.go`: TSDB NewDB() function creates and registers metrics for the database instance\\n   - `storage/remote/queue_manager.go`: Queue manager creates histogram and counter metrics during initialization\\n   - `discovery/manager.go`: Discovery manager creates gauges and counters for scrape targets\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Abstraction Level**: Kubernetes > Grafana > Prometheus (in terms of abstraction from raw Prometheus client library)\\n\\n2. **Dependency Injection**: \\n   - Kubernetes: Primarily uses global/package-level registries\\n   - Grafana: Heavy use of dependency injection for registerers\\n   - Prometheus: Direct Prometheus client usage, some parameter-based registry passing\\n\\n3. **Metric Lifecycle**:\\n   - Kubernetes: Metrics created at package init() time and registered to global or injected registries\\n   - Grafana: Metrics created in NewService() constructors with injected registerers\\n   - Prometheus: Metrics created during component initialization with MustRegister()\\n\\n4. **Naming Conventions**:\\n   - Kubernetes: Uses component-base prefix system (e.g., \\\"apiserver_\\\", \\\"kubelet_\\\")\\n   - Grafana: Uses service-specific prefixes injected via WrapRegistererWithPrefix()\\n   - Prometheus: Uses flat naming with component prefixes (e.g., \\\"prometheus_tsdb_\\\", \\\"prometheus_discovery_\\\")\\n\\n### Common Patterns Across All Three\\n\\n1. **MustRegister() Pattern**: All three use MustRegister() as the primary registration mechanism, which panics on duplicate metric registration, preventing accidental metric name collisions.\\n\\n2. **Metric Types**: All three implement the same metric types using the Prometheus Go client library:\\n   - Counters for monotonically increasing values\\n   - Gauges for values that can increase or decrease\\n   - Histograms for distribution measurements\\n   - Some use Summaries for quantile calculations\\n\\n3. **Labels/Tags**: All three use labels (called dimensions in some contexts) for cardinality and filtering.\\n\\n4. **Init-Time Registration**: All metrics are registered at package/component initialization time, not at runtime, for performance and safety.\\n\\nThis comparison reveals that while all three projects use the same underlying Prometheus Go client library, they differ significantly in architectural approach: Kubernetes abstracts the metrics layer for consistency and control, Grafana uses dependency injection for flexibility, and Prometheus uses direct client integration for simplicity.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1467,"cache_read_input_tokens":27571,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1467},"output_tokens":7,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d90d4133-ef04-4fec-b8c7-786e89eb2d50","uuid":"51564ad9-388d-478b-9852-208331dcf5e9"}

histograms, gauges) are registered and exposed across three major projects: kubernetes/kubernetes, grafana/grafana, and prometheus/prometheus.\\n\\n### Kubernetes/Kubernetes Pattern\\n\\nKubernetes implements a centralized metrics framework in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/` that abstracts away direct Prometheus dependencies. Key characteristics:\\n\\n1. **Central Registry Abstraction**: `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go` defines a `KubeRegistry` interface that wraps Prometheus registries with custom validation and deprecation tracking. This allows Kubernetes to add custom business logic around metric registration.\\n\\n2. **Legacy Registry Pattern**: `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go` provides a global registry using `RawMustRegister()` for backward compatibility, while newer code uses injected registry instances.\\n\\n3. **Metric Type Wrappers**: Counter, Gauge, and Histogram creation is abstracted through `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/counter.go`, `gauge.go`, and `histogram.go`. These wrappers call `prometheus.NewCounter()`, `prometheus.NewGauge()`, and `prometheus.NewHistogram()` respectively, but add Kubernetes-specific validation.\\n\\n4. **Component-Level Registration**: Each component (controllers, api-server, kubelet, scheduler, proxy) has its own metrics file (e.g., `pkg/controller/cronjob/metrics/metrics.go`, `pkg/scheduler/metrics/metrics.go`) that initializes metrics in init() functions and registers them with either the legacy registry or a KubeRegistry instance. Controllers use `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` while newer components use injected registries.\\n\\n### Grafana/Grafana Pattern\\n\\nGrafana uses a more distributed approach with dependency injection:\\n\\n1. **Metrics Service**: `pkg/infra/metrics/service.go` provides a `MetricsService` that manages prometheus.Registerer and prometheus.Gatherer instances. This service is injected into components that need to register metrics.\\n\\n2. **Distributed Registration**: Unlike Kubernetes's centralized component directories, Grafana's metrics are scattered throughout the codebase. Each service that needs metrics (alerts, dashboards, authentication, storage, etc.) has its own metrics file that receives an injected `prometheus.Registerer` as a dependency.\\n\\n3. **Registration Methods**:\\n   - Direct: `prometheus.MustRegister()` for global metrics\\n   - Injected: `registerer.MustRegister()` for service-specific metrics\\n   - Automatic: `promauto.With(registerer).New*()` for automatic registration with injected registerer\\n   - Conditional: `registerer.Register()` with error handling\\n\\n4. **Examples**:\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/ngalert.go`: NGAlert metrics factory receives a `prometheus.Registerer`\\n   - `pkg/services/dashboards/service/metrics.go`: Dashboard metrics use injected registerer\\n   - `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/metrics.go`: Authentication metrics with dependency injection\\n   - `pkg/services/secrets/manager/metrics.go`: Secrets manager metrics\\n   - `pkg/middleware/request_metrics.go`: HTTP middleware metrics\\n\\n5. **Namespace/Prefix Pattern**: Many Grafana services use `prometheus.WrapRegistererWithPrefix()` to add namespaced prefixes to metrics, creating logical grouping (e.g., \\\"grafana_alerting_\\\", \\\"grafana_dashboard_\\\").\\n\\n### Prometheus/Prometheus Pattern\\n\\nPrometheus itself uses an embedded metrics pattern:\\n\\n1. **No Central Abstraction**: Unlike Kubernetes, Prometheus directly uses the Prometheus Go client library throughout the codebase. There's no intermediate wrapper layer.\\n\\n2. **Distributed Component Metrics**: Metrics are registered in individual components:\\n   - `discovery/metrics.go`: Generic discovery metrics\\n   - `discovery/{consul,dns,kubernetes}/metrics.go`: Service discovery provider-specific metrics\\n   - `scrape/metrics.go`: Scrape manager metrics\\n   - `storage/remote/`: Remote storage client and queue manager metrics\\n   - `tsdb/{db.go,head.go,agent/db.go}`: Time-series database metrics\\n   - `rules/manager.go`: Rule evaluation metrics\\n   - `notifier/metric.go`: Alert notification metrics\\n   - `web/web.go`: HTTP API metrics\\n\\n3. **Registration Pattern**: Each component creates metrics in init() or NewComponent() functions and immediately registers them with `prometheus.MustRegister()` or `registry.MustRegister()` (where registry is passed as parameter or created locally).\\n\\n4. **Examples of Registration**:\\n   - `cmd/prometheus/main.go`: Main process initialization registers all component metrics\\n   - `tsdb/db.go`: TSDB NewDB() function creates and registers metrics for the database instance\\n   - `storage/remote/queue_manager.go`: Queue manager creates histogram and counter metrics during initialization\\n   - `discovery/manager.go`: Discovery manager creates gauges and counters for scrape targets\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Abstraction Level**: Kubernetes > Grafana > Prometheus (in terms of abstraction from raw Prometheus client library)\\n\\n2. **Dependency Injection**: \\n   - Kubernetes: Primarily uses global/package-level registries\\n   - Grafana: Heavy use of dependency injection for registerers\\n   - Prometheus: Direct Prometheus client usage, some parameter-based registry passing\\n\\n3. **Metric Lifecycle**:\\n   - Kubernetes: Metrics created at package init() time and registered to global or injected registries\\n   - Grafana: Metrics created in NewService() constructors with injected registerers\\n   - Prometheus: Metrics created during component initialization with MustRegister()\\n\\n4. **Naming Conventions**:\\n   - Kubernetes: Uses component-base prefix system (e.g., \\\"apiserver_\\\", \\\"kubelet_\\\")\\n   - Grafana: Uses service-specific prefixes injected via WrapRegistererWithPrefix()\\n   - Prometheus: Uses flat naming with component prefixes (e.g., \\\"prometheus_tsdb_\\\", \\\"prometheus_discovery_\\\")\\n\\n### Common Patterns Across All Three\\n\\n1. **MustRegister() Pattern**: All three use MustRegister() as the primary registration mechanism, which panics on duplicate metric registration, preventing accidental metric name collisions.\\n\\n2. **Metric Types**: All three implement the same metric types using the Prometheus Go client library:\\n   - Counters for monotonically increasing values\\n   - Gauges for values that can increase or decrease\\n   - Histograms for distribution measurements\\n   - Some use Summaries for quantile calculations\\n\\n3. **Labels/Tags**: All three use labels (called dimensions in some contexts) for cardinality and filtering.\\n\\n4. **Init-Time Registration**: All metrics are registered at package/component initialization time, not at runtime, for performance and safety.\\n\\nThis comparison reveals that while all three projects use the same underlying Prometheus Go client library, they differ significantly in architectural approach: Kubernetes abstracts the metrics layer for consistency and control, Grafana uses dependency injection for flexibility, and Prometheus uses direct client integration for simplicity.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
